# PeaMac Tees (https://peamactees.com)

- Domain: https://peamactees.com
- Locale: en
- Currency: USD
- Timezone: America/New_York
- Created At: 2025-11-16T02:56:27Z
- Contact Email: support@peamactees.com
- Updated At: 2026-04-25T19:33:45.876Z

PeaMacTees is a Canadian online apparel brand offering fun, expressive, and giftable graphic t-shirts and accessories. Our collections focus on hobbies, lifestyle passions, and feel-good self-expression, including pickleball, pets, positivity themes, and playful personality statements.

Products include unisex and youth t-shirts, tote bags, hats, drinkware, and small accessories designed for everyday wear and thoughtful gifting. PeaMacTees emphasizes comfort, lighthearted design, and inclusive sizing. Many items are especially popular as gifts for active adults, hobby enthusiasts, and community-minded shoppers.

The official website is https://www.peamactees.com
 where customers can browse all collections and purchase directly.

Bright, pop-art energy meets sporty function: the neon yellow pickleball replaces the “O” in a bold LOVE graphic, so the moment you walk onto the court or into a café everyone knows where your loyalties lie. The soft, Airlume combed and ring-spun cotton feels smooth against skin during long rallies and cooldowns. Thoughtful construction — side seams, shoulder tape, and a ribbed knit collar — keeps the shirt holding its shape match after match. Wear it with your paddle bag, visor, and court shoes for league nights, tournament weekends, or casual meetups with your doubles crew. Ethically produced in sustainable,  facilities and finished with a tear-away label for comfort, this tee is built for players who want style, durability, and a little playful swagger in their game.Product features- 100% Airlume combed and ring-spun cotton for a soft, lightweight feel (Heather blends vary).- Side seams and shoulder tape for improved shape retention and structural support.- Ribbed knit collar with seam for elastic recovery and a neat crew neckline.- Produced in sustainable,  facilities (Fair Labor Association, Platinum WRAP); REACH .- Tear-away label to minimize skin irritation; available sleeve and neck printing via DTF or DTG, depending on provider. - [Classic Pickleball Tee — "Pickleball" Script Design](https://peamactees.com/products/classic-pickleball-tee-pickleball-script-design): Lightweight, breathable, and quietly confident — this classic pickleball shirt brings the calm energy of the court into everyday life. The white script “Pickleball” with a subtle wave underline and tiny paddle and ball icons reads like a nod between players: familiar, understated, and a little nostalgic. It sits soft against the skin thanks to Airlume combed and ring-spun cotton, and the retail crew neckline keeps the silhouette clean whether you’re serving, spectating, or grabbing a post-game coffee. Ethically made materials and water-based inks mean the tee wears easy and feels right — like showing up to the court as yourself, with a small, proud smile.Product features- 100% Airlume combed & ring-spun cotton — lightweight 4.2 oz fabric for breathable comfort- White script print with retro wave and small paddle/pickleball icons using eco-friendly, water-based inks- Constructed with side seams, ribbed knit collar, shoulder tape, and retail crew neckline for a lasting shape- Tear-away label and REACH certification; sourced blank from Honduras with ethical manufacturing standards- Available color blends (heather/ash variations) and sleeve/label printing done with crisp DTF or vibrant DTG methods Unisex Sizing: XS S M L XL 2XL 3XL 4XL Width, in 16.50 18.00 20.00 22.00 24.00 26.00 28.00 30.00 Length, in 27.00 28.00 29.00 30.00 31.00 32.00 33.00 34.00 Sleeve length, in 8.60 8.90 9.20 9.50 9.70 10.00 10.40 10.80 Size tolerance, in 1.50 1.50 1.50 1.50 1.50 1.50 1.50 1.50 EU representative: PeaMac Tees, support@peamactees.com, 415 Jarvis St, Mod 6 Comp 9, Toronto, ON, M4Y 3C1, CA Product information: Bella+Canvas 3001, 2 year warranty in EU and Northern Ireland as per Directive 1999/44/EC Warnings, Hazard: For adults, Blank product sourced from Honduras Care instructions: Machine wash: cold (max 30C or 90F), Non-chlorine: bleach as needed, Tumble dry: low heat, Iron, steam or dry: medium heat, Do not dryclean

Wearers will find themselves slipping into the calm of a misty Pacific Northwest shoreline, paddle-ready but relaxed. The design reads as a tranquil landscape from across the room, then reveals a tucked-away pickleball court to fellow players and island lovers — a gentle nod to community, outdoor play, and shoreline afternoons. Lightweight and breathable, the shirt moves easily from pre-game warmups and league nights to coffee runs and trail-side strolls. This slim, two-piece phone case pairs a tough polycarbonate shell with a flexible TPU liner to guard against drops while keeping a clean, glossy look. On a deep navy field, a pixelated pickleball streaks and fragments in red, orange, yellow, and blue — playful, bright, and a little nostalgic. It lies flat to protect screen edges, resists UV fading so the colors hold up in sunlight, and slips easily into pockets or bags. Lightweight but resilient, it supports wireless charging and now fits the latest iPhone 17 models, so your phone stays protected without losing function.
